## Text Elements
Local minimum  ^qI8fa4MH

Local maximum ^MMIAqwCy

Find the turning point of: ^4fhmtPo8

Find the least value of: ^jEdRWAM1

A point of inflection is where the curve changes from convex concave (or vice versa) ^VA9XcwM4

i.e the line curves in one direction before the point of inflection, then in the other direction. ^pkYz04wW

Find the coordinates of the turning points of  ^Vv8Yb1md

At a stationary point x = a:
- if f''(a) > 0 the point is a local minimum.
- if f''(a) < 0 the point is a local maximum.
- if f''(a) = 0 it could be any type of point, so resort to method 1. ^ugrFzt1a

At a maximum point, we can see that as x increases, the gradient is deceasing from a positive value to a negative value. ^2xMlCPd5

Find the stationary point on the curve with equation                            , and determine whether it is a local maximum, a local minimum, or a point of inflection. ^Blgmn6rM
